           const el = document.getElementById(id);\r\n            if (!el) return;\r\n\r\n            el.classList.remove(\"positive\", \"negative\");\r\n\r\n            if (id === \"m-symbol\" || id === \"m-price\" || id === \"m-equity\") {\r\n                el.textContent = value;\r\n                return;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            if (id === \"maxdd\") {\r\n                el.style.color = \"#000000\";\r\n                if (typeof value === \"string\" && value.startsWith(\"-\")) {\r\n                    el.style.color = \"#d00000\";\r\n                }\r\n                el.textContent = value;\r\n                return;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            if (typeof value === \"string\" && value.startsWith(\"-\")) {\r\n                el.classList.add(\"negative\");\r\n            } else if (typeof value === \"string\" && value !== \"-\" && value !== \"0\" && !value.startsWith(\"0.\")) {\r\n                el.classList.add(\"positive\");\r\n            }\r\n            el.textContent = value;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatNumber(v, digits = 2) {\r\n            if (v === null || v === undefined || isNaN(v)) return \"-\";\r\n            return Number(v).toLocaleString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                minimumFractionDigits: digits,\r\n                maximumFractionDigits: digits,\r\n            });\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatPercent(v, digits = 2) {\r\n            if (v === null || v === undefined || isNaN(v)) return \"-\";\r\n            return (Number(v) * 100).toFixed(digits) + \"%\";\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatTimeLabel(ts) {\r\n            try {\r\n                const d = new Date(ts);\r\n                if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return String(ts ?? \"\");\r\n                return d.toLocaleTimeString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                    hour12: false,\r\n                    hour: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    minute: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    second: \"2-digit\",\r\n                });\r\n            } catch {\r\n                return String(ts ?? \"\");\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ ë²„í¼ =====\r\n        let maxPoints = 300;\r\n\r\n        const labelsHist = [];\r\n        const equityHist = [];\r\n        const priceHist = [];\r\n        const posHist = [];\r\n        const ddHist = [];\r\n        const ddWarnHist = [];\r\n        const ddCutHist = [];\r\n        const cumPnlHist = [];\r\n        const buyMarkersHist = [];\r\n        const sellMarkersHist = [];\r\n\r\n        // BUY / SELL ë§ˆì»¤ ê³„ì‚°ìš© ìƒíƒœ\r\n        let lastPos = null;\r\n\r\n        const BUY_MARK_Y = 0.4;\r\n        const SELL_MARK_Y = 0.6;\r\n\r\n        function trimHistoryArrays() {\r\n            const arrays = [\r\n                labelsHist,\r\n                equityHist,\r\n                priceHist,\r\n                posHist,\r\n                ddHist,\r\n                cumPnlHist,\r\n                buyMarkersHist,\r\n                sellMarkersHist,\r\n            ];\r\n\r\n            arrays.forEach(arr => {\r\n                if (arr.length > maxPoints) {\r\n                    arr.splice(0, arr.length - maxPoints);\r\n                }\r\n            });\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function pushHistoryPoint(data) {\r\n            const nowTs = data.ts || data.time || new Date().toISOString();\r\n\r\n            const label = formatTimeLabel(nowTs);\r\n            const price = Number(data.price ?? data.px ?? 0);\r\n            const equity = Number(data.equity ?? data.eq ?? 0);\r\n            const pos = Number(data.position ?? data.pos ?? 0);\r\n            const ddRaw = Number(data.dd ?? data.drawdown ?? 0);\r\n            const cumPnl = Number(data.cum_pnl ?? data.cumpnl ?? data.pnl_cum ?? data.rpnl ?? 0);\r\n\r\n            let ddVal = ddRaw;\r\n            if (Math.abs(ddVal) > 1) ddVal = ddVal / 100.0;\r\n\r\n            labelsHist.push(label);\r\n            priceHist.push(price);\r\n            equityHist.push(equity);\r\n            posHist.push(pos);\r\n            ddHist.push(ddVal);\r\n\r\n            ddWarnHist.push(Number(data.dd_warn ?? 0));\r\n            ddCutHist.push(Number(data.dd_cut ?? 0));\r\n\r\n            cumPnlHist.push(cumPnl);\r\n\r\n            // ==== BUY/SELL ë§ˆì»¤: í¬ì§€ì…˜ ë³€í™” ê°ì§€ ====\r\n            let buyMark = null;\r\n            let sellMark = null;\r\n\r\n            const EPS = 0.00000001; // ê·¹ì†ŒëŸ‰ ë…¸ì´ì¦ˆëŠ” ë¬´ì‹œ\r\n\r\n            if (lastPos === null) {\r\n                lastPos = pos;\r\n            } else {\r\n                const diffPos = pos - lastPos;\r\n\r\n                if (Math.abs(diffPos) > EPS) {\r\n                    if (diffPos > 0) {\r\n                        buyMark = BUY_MARK_Y;\r\n                    } else {\r\n                        sellMark = SELL_MARK_Y;\r\n                    }\r\n                    lastPos = pos;\r\n                }\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            buyMarkersHist.push(buyMark);\r\n            sellMarkersHist.push(sellMark);\r\n\r\n            trimHistoryArrays();\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ì°¨íŠ¸ ê°ì²´ =====\r\n        let mainChart = null;\r\n        let pnlChart = null;\r\n\r\n        // ===== ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ· + ì°¨íŠ¸ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ =====\r\n        function updateSnapshotAndCharts(data) {\r\n            const symbol = data.symbol ?? \"-\";\r\n            const price = data.price ?? null;\r\n            const pos = data.position ?? null;\r\n            const eq = data.equity ?? null;\r\n            const rpnl = data.rpnl ?? 0;\r\n            const upnl = data.upnl ?? 0;\r\n            const dd = data.dd ?? null;\r\n            const maxdd = data.max_dd ?? null;\r\n            const totalPnl = (rpnl || 0) + (upnl || 0);\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-symbol\", symbol);\r\n            setMetric(\"m-price\", formatNumber(price));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-position\", formatNumber(pos, 4));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-equity\", formatNumber(eq));\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-pnl\", formatNumber(totalPnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-upnl\", formatNumber(upnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-rpnl\", formatNumber(rpnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-cumpnl\", formatNumber(data.cum_pnl ?? totalPnl));\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-dd\", formatPercent(dd));\r\n            setMetric(\"maxdd\", formatPercent(maxdd));\r\n\r\n            const lu = document.getElementById(\"last-updated\");\r\n            if (lu) {\r\n                lu.textContent =\r\n                    \"Last update: \" +\r\n                    new Date().toLocaleTimeString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                        hour12: false,\r\n                        hour: \"2-digit\",\r\n                        minute: \"2-digit\",\r\n                        second: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    });\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ + ì°¨íŠ¸ ë°˜ì˜\r\n            pushHistoryPoint(data);\r\n\r\n            if (!mainChart || !pnlChart) return;\r\n\r\n            mainChart.data.labels = [...labelsHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[0].data = [...equityHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[1].data = [...priceHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[2].data = [...cumPnlHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[3].data = [...buyMarkersHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[4].data = [...sellMarkersHist];\r\n            mainChart.update();\r\n\r\n            pnlChart.data.labels = [...labelsHist];\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[0].data = [...posHist];\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[1].data = [...ddHist];\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[2].data = [...ddWarnHist];\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[3].data = [...ddCutHist];\r\n            pnlChart.update();\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ í—¬í¼ =====\r\n        async function fetchRiskProfileStatus() {\r\n            try {\r\n                const resp = await fetch(\"/api/risk-profile/active\");\r\n                if (!resp.ok) {\r\n                    console.error(\"[RISK_PROFILE] fetch ì‹¤íŒ¨\", resp.status);\r\n                    return null;\r\n                }\r\n                return await resp.json();\r\n\r\n            } catch (err) {\r\n                console.error(\"[RISK_PROFILE] fetch ì—ëŸ¬\", err);\r\n                return null;\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        async function refreshRiskProfileUI() {\r\n            const data = await fetchRiskProfileStatus();\r\n            if (!data) return;\r\n\r\n            const select = document.getElementById(\"risk-profile-select\");\r\n            const label = document.getElementById(\"active-risk-profile\");\r\n\r\n            // 1) ì—”ì§„ ê¸°ì¤€ì´ â€œì§„ì§œ ê°’â€\r\n            const engineActive =\r\n                data.engine_active_profile ||\r\n                \"neutral\";\r\n\r\n            // 2) UI ê°’ì€ ì—”ì§„ ì—†ì„ ë•Œë§Œ ë³´ì¡°ë¡œ ì‚¬ìš©\r\n            const uiActive = data.ui_active_profile || engineActive;\r\n\r\n            // ğŸ”¹ ì½¤ë³´ë°•ìŠ¤ëŠ” í•­ìƒ ì—”ì§„ ê°’ì— ë§ì¶˜ë‹¤\r\n            if (select) {\r\n                select.value = engineActive;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // ğŸ”¹ ë¼ë²¨ë„ ì—”ì§„ ê°’ ê¸°ì¤€ìœ¼ë¡œ í‘œì‹œ\r\n            if (label) {\r\n                const nameMap = {\r\n                    conservative: \"ë³´ìˆ˜í˜•\",\r\n                    neutral: \"ì¤‘ë¦½í˜•\",\r\n                    aggressive: \"ê³µê²©í˜•\",\r\n                };\r\n                label.textContent =\r\n                    `í˜„ì¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼: ${nameMap[engineActive] || engineActive}`;\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ· ìƒˆë¡œê³ ì¹¨ =====\r\n        async function refreshSnapshot() {\r\n            try {\r\n                const res = await fetch(\"/api/snapshot\");\r\n                if (!res.ok) throw new Error(\"snapshot http \" + res.status);\r\n\r\n                const data = await res.json();\r\n                window.snapshot_last = data;\r\n\r\n                const banner = document.getElementById(\"alert-banner\");\r\n                const snap = document.querySelector(\"section.card.snapshot\");\r\n\r\n                if (!banner || !snap) return;   // âœ… ì—¬ê¸° ì¶”ê°€ (banner.className ì „ì—)\r\n\r\n                banner.className = \"alert-banner hidden\";\r\n                snap.classList.remove(\"warn-border\", \"cut-border\");\r\n\r\n                if (data.alert_level === \"WARN\") {\r\n                    banner.textContent = \"âš  DD WARN\";\r\n                    banner.classList.remove(\"hidden\");\r\n                    banner.classList.add(\"warn\");\r\n                    snap.classList.add(\"warn-border\");\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                if (data.alert_level === \"CUT\") {\r\n                    banner.textContent = \"ğŸš¨ DD CUT\";\r\n                    banner.classList.remove(\"hidden\");\r\n                    banner.classList.add(\"cut\");\r\n                    snap.classList.add(\"cut-border\");\r\n                }\r\n\r\n\r\n                const level = (data.alert_level || \"OK\").toUpperCase();\r\n                const cls =\r\n                    level === \"CUT\" ? \"level-cut\" :\r\n                        level === \"WARN\" ? \"level-warn\" :\r\n                            \"level-ok\";\r\n\r\n                [\"m-dd\", \"m-dd-warn\", \"m-dd-cut\", \"m-alert-level\"].forEach(id => {\r\n                    const el = document.getElementById(id);\r\n                    if (!el) return;\r\n                    el.classList.remove(\"level-ok\", \"level-warn\", \"level-cut\");\r\n                    el.classList.add(cls);\r\n                });\r\n\r\n                // âœ… í•„ìš”í•˜ë©´ ë‹¤ë¥¸ ê³³ì—ì„œ ì¨ë„ ë˜ë„ë¡ ì „ì—­ì— ì €ì¥\r\n                window.snapshot_last = data;\r\n\r\n                // ğŸ”¢ DD / WARN / CUT / ALERT ê°’ ì„¸íŒ…\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd-warn\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd_warn * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd-cut\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd_cut * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-alert-level\").innerText =\r\n                    data.alert_level || \"-\";\r\n\r\n\r\n                // ìƒë‹¨ ì¹´ë“œ + ì°¨íŠ¸ ê°±ì‹ \r\n                updateSnapshotAndCharts(data);\r\n\r\n                // âœ… ë¹„ìš© íŒ¨ë„ì€ ì „ì²´ ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ·(data)ì„ ë„˜ê¸´ë‹¤\r\n                updateCostMetricsPanel(data);\r\n\r\n            } catch (err) {\r\n                console.error(\"snapshot error\", err);\r\n                const lu = document.getElementById(\"last-updated\");\r\n                if (lu) lu.textContent = \"ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ· ì˜¤ë¥˜\";\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n\r\n        // ===== ë¹„ìš© íŒ¨ë„ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ =====\r\n        function updateCostMetricsPanel(snapshot) {\r\n            if (!snapshot) return;\r\n\r\n            // âœ… ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ·ì—ì„œ cost_metrics êº¼ë‚´ê¸°\r\n            const cm = snapshot.cost_metrics || {};\r\n\r\n            function put(id, value, digits = 2) {\r\n                const el = document.getElementById(id);\r\n                if (!el) return;\r\n                if (value === null || value === undefined || isNaN(value)) {\r\n                    el.textContent = \"-\";\r\n                    return;\r\n                }\r\n                el.textContent = Number(value).toFixed(digits);\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // âœ… ìµœê·¼ Nê±´ í‰ê·  ê°œìˆ˜ N (ì„¤ì • íŒŒì¼ì˜ cost_window ìš°ì„ , ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ë‚´ë¶€ maxlen)\r\n            const nWindow =\r\n                snapshot.cost_window ??\r\n                cm.rolling_window_maxlen ??\r\n                0;\r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-size\", nWindow, 0);\r\n            put(\"m-risk-mult\", snapshot.risk_mult, 4);\r\n            put(\"m-dyn-max-pos\", snapshot.dyn_max_pos, 6);\r\n\r\n            // ìµœê·¼ ì²´ê²°\r\n            put(\"cost-last-total\", cm.last_total_cost_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-last-slippage\", cm.last_slippage_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-last-fee\", cm.last_fee_bps, 2);\r\n\r\n            // ì„¸ì…˜ ëˆ„ì \r\n            put(\"cost-session-total-sum\", cm.session_total_cost_sum, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-session-slip-sum\", cm.session_slippage_sum, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-session-fee-sum\", cm.session_fee_sum, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-session-trade-count\", cm.session_trade_count, 0);\r\n\r\n            // ìµœê·¼ Nê±´ í‰ê· \r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-total\", cm.rolling_total_cost_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-slip\", cm.rolling_slippage_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-fee\", cm.rolling_fee_bps, 2);\r\n        }\r\n\r\n\r\n        // ===== window load =====\r\n        window.addEventListener(\"load\", async () => {\r\n            // ğŸ”¹ ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ ì½¤ë³´ DOM\r\n            const riskSelect =
